  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1a3587da-1bdf-406d-a459-0b84c27170fc'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText9459365807416752522" style="display:none">Arianna Calin has sworn to keep the peace in Riverdale. Most of the Otherworlders prefer to haunt the Olde Town district--partying at vampire strip clubs, dining in elegant supper clubs, and inhabiting the cliffside caverns along the Mississippi. Being a cop is a tough job, but someone's gotta do it, and Ari's got her derringer, a sharp stiletto, and a few handy charms against things that hunt in the night. She's also a fire witch--a pedigree that comes in handy, since her partner's only human.<br /><br />When a virtual reality drug hits the streets, people start to die, and an elusive pack of werewolves threatens the status quo. Ari and Ryan are drawn into a web of murder and evil that will lead sworn enemies to a confrontation. While the city simmers around them, Ari struggles to prevent an all-out supernatural war...</span>

<div id="review_926422204" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/926422204" />
    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/926422204?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19444019-awakening-the-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-romance">pn-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-shapeshifters">pn-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-vampires">pn-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-witches-magic">pn-witches-magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=first-in-series">first-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer926422204" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4603832513919762847"><i>My casting:</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405905013i/10468728.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The book follows Arianna Calin who is a Guardian in Riverdale, Olde Town. She's young and talented. Strong and independent. She also has powerful power, fire. Yup, you guessed it, Ari is a fire witch. Which comes in handy considering she's up against vampires, werewolves, and a whole lot more Otherworlders, and on top of that, her partner, Lt. Ryan Foster, is only human. On her first big mission, she has to solve a mysterious case were people die, werewolves makes trouble and a drug c</span>
  <span id="freeText4603832513919762847" style="display:none"><i>My casting:</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405905013i/10468728.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The book follows Arianna Calin who is a Guardian in Riverdale, Olde Town. She's young and talented. Strong and independent. She also has powerful power, fire. Yup, you guessed it, Ari is a fire witch. Which comes in handy considering she's up against vampires, werewolves, and a whole lot more Otherworlders, and on top of that, her partner, Lt. Ryan Foster, is only human. On her first big mission, she has to solve a mysterious case were people die, werewolves makes trouble and a drug called 'Fantasty' hits the street, someone is trying to control the vampires.. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>As Ari watched his dark head bend over the door, silent amusement bubbled in her throat. The ever-so-cool Mr. De Luca was acting as if he didn’t trust himself. Probably a good thing, she thought. Deep inside, she was feeling very smug. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>While being on a patrolling she meets the powerful and mysterious Andreas De Luca. A vampire who seems to be more than he lets people think he is. His and Ari's magic seem to, how to say this, connect, which frightens Ari. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ari brought her chin up. She hated it when someone told her what to do. Or even worse, what she couldn’t do. “You keep forgetting I can take care of myself.”<br>“So you’ve said before. But it would be better to stay out of situations where you might have to prove it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ally Shields writes in a phenomenal way were you get to connect and grown with the characters. She writes in a way that you feel that your a part of the book, were you have to solve the cases. That fact that she can make a fantastic book were there are none love triangles, is just great. I hate love triangles and to be honest, I was afraid that this book would have exactly that, but lucky me, it didn't :D I loved how she describes how the humans and the otherworlders were able to live together in somewhat peace. The dynamics and tension between everyone.. It all just worked.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t want to get better. That’s the problem.” Ari didn’t bother to hide the confusion she felt. “I want to stay angry. Need the anger. I’m going to find them and kill them.” Ari looked at her friend’s shocked face. “Does that make me as bad as they are?” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>A great start on a series :)! I love it! &lt;3 The characters were awesome, and Andreas was freaking awesome! I love that this book didn't have insta-love and that you fall in love with the characters while Ari falls in love with them. Ari was just the type of character that I love. She so independent woman. She tough, smart and snarky but has so much emotions inside that she refuses to show anyone. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406152137ra/10511782.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So in a way she's vulnerable, and I love it. I just hope that she let's someone in, and with that someone i mean <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Andreas <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Ari's very loyal and goes by an oath which she refuses to break. She has to go through some tough things that can break a weak person, but luckily she takes all that pain and anger and makes it to a good thing. Andreas is just.. my man! I love him, and I want more!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406152452ra/10511823.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't wait to read more about Ari and Andreas. Though the series reminds me of Anita Blake series by Laurell K. Hamilton, it's great. To be honest, I kinda like this book more than I did A.B series.. The things I didn't like was that things were a bit slow, and I wish more had happened. Other than that, the book was great and I can't wait to read more! :)<br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4603832513919762847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1257253126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10138361694573055879">Awakening the Fire by Ally Shields is captivating, well written and full of action. I instantly connected with the characters and the intrigue kept me turning the pages to see what happened next. The beginning is a little slow but once you get beyond that, the plot moves quickly.<br/><br/>My Rating: 4.5 stars</span>

<div id="review_460928344" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/460928344" />
    <a title="Brinda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4441791-brinda"><img alt="Brinda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1478195181p2/4441791.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/460928344?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brinda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brinda" href="/user/show/4441791-brinda">Brinda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460928344" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3203652819566914203">When I first began reading this book, I was reminded of all the things I loved about the first two Anita Blake (Laurell K. Hamilton) books. Ari, the heroine, is somebody you can root for in a book. She's committed to her job, smart as a whip, and vulnerable to a sexy guy. When I say vulnerable, I mean that you can sense her attraction to the powerful vampire in town. It doesn't mean she jumped into bed after meeting him. I loved the tension. <br/><br/>I also felt like this book was similar to watching CSI</span>
  <span id="freeText3203652819566914203" style="display:none">When I first began reading this book, I was reminded of all the things I loved about the first two Anita Blake (Laurell K. Hamilton) books. Ari, the heroine, is somebody you can root for in a book. She's committed to her job, smart as a whip, and vulnerable to a sexy guy. When I say vulnerable, I mean that you can sense her attraction to the powerful vampire in town. It doesn't mean she jumped into bed after meeting him. I loved the tension. <br /><br />I also felt like this book was similar to watching CSI (which I love). There are twists, interesting suspects, and murders to solve. Although it's a paranormal, Shields does a terrific job of making it seem normal to hang out with a witch and vampires. There are other supernatural creatures as well, but Shields doesn't belabor the descriptions. <br /><br />Ally Shields is an author to watch. I try to take off my writer's cap while reading for pleasure. It's difficult. I can honestly say that I am in awe of her skill in subtle world-building, snappy and entertaining dialogue, and characters I grew to love. Speaking of dialogue, I laughed a lot at the humorous interactions between Ari and the other characters. Shields is highly quotable. <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3203652819566914203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirstin Pulioff" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirstin Pulioff" href="/user/show/11281401-kirstin-pulioff">Kirstin Pulioff</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424043013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16020280378355676656">I just had the honor of reading Ally Shield’s “Awakening the Fire,” and it lived up to its name. It awakened all my senses and left me waiting for more. This story is an amazing piece of art, weaving the characters, relationships, plots, backstories and drama into a masterpiece.<br/><br/>Ally has a wonderful way with words, describing her characters with such depth and ease, that you truly feel like you are there in the story. The connection and pull between the characters is palatable. From the different</span>
  <span id="freeText16020280378355676656" style="display:none">I just had the honor of reading Ally Shield’s “Awakening the Fire,” and it lived up to its name. It awakened all my senses and left me waiting for more. This story is an amazing piece of art, weaving the characters, relationships, plots, backstories and drama into a masterpiece.<br /><br />Ally has a wonderful way with words, describing her characters with such depth and ease, that you truly feel like you are there in the story. The connection and pull between the characters is palatable. From the different dynamics between the vampires, itches, werewolves and humans, to the forbidden desire between the characters, a wide range of feelings is explored. This is a story that draws you in, invests your feelings in their relationships and outcomes, and does not disappoint in the twists and turns.<br /><br />Her fantasy world is clearly defined, and imaginable. The boundaries between the mystical and the human are concrete, and the cohesion of the two worlds very natural. This is a place you know, a town set up in a manner you are familiar with. The clubs, the park, the town, all places that you can relate to and imagine being in.<br /><br />The premise of the story is original, and suspenseful. I was on the edge of my seat the entire time. Completely hooked from page one, I am eagerly awaiting the next in this series. Overall, the highest rating I can give it. Fantastic book.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16020280378355676656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_422407009" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/422407009?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peter Jenkins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peter Jenkins" href="/user/show/5960699-peter-jenkins">Peter Jenkins</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer422407009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13797154672125944748">Some authors imagine they can copy the style of a genre such as the fantasy world inhabited by witches, vampires, werewolves and the like, but only manage to fool a few of their readers. Not so Ally Shields who has truly mastered the occult nuances of fantasy, and, gathered together the ingredients for a sound, fast moving plot. She has added her considerable flair as a wordsmith: descriptions in the opening pages of the book were stunning. Awakening the Fire is a genuinely exciting story that f</span>
  <span id="freeText13797154672125944748" style="display:none">Some authors imagine they can copy the style of a genre such as the fantasy world inhabited by witches, vampires, werewolves and the like, but only manage to fool a few of their readers. Not so Ally Shields who has truly mastered the occult nuances of fantasy, and, gathered together the ingredients for a sound, fast moving plot. She has added her considerable flair as a wordsmith: descriptions in the opening pages of the book were stunning. Awakening the Fire is a genuinely exciting story that focuses on Ari the beautiful witch who has been appointed a Guardian by her otherworld community. We’ve hardly begun the story when a violent attack on two teens by a werewolf is foiled by her immediate response on their behalf. Immediately the author wastes no time to introduce Andreas, the sexy but dangerous vampire who features in the story. From there we move from one-attention grabbing event after another. Andreas turning on the charm, Andreas verbally dueling with Ryan the human policeman in a verbal dual with Andreas, the “collaborator” he does not trust. There was a point when I agreed with Sheila that recriminations could have been less frequent, but the sheer pace of the tale, Ari’s audacity that took her through confrontation after skirmish, to the all out attack on Prince Daron’’s encampment convinced me that here was a writing talent that deserves full marks. But don’t ask me how I stopped the blood dripping from my fangs as I read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13797154672125944748" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4374163759268634577" style="display:none">NOTE: I received this book from the author/publisher in exchange for a review.<br /><br />Ari (Arianna) Calin is a guardian in the riverfront section of Riverdale. A city where humans and otherworlders, vampires, werewolves, witches and others co-exist to an extent. She handles anything to do with magic or the otherworlders and her human partner Lt. Ryan Foster the human side of it. The story starts with Ari patrolling when she heard screams and comes upon a teen couple trying to ward off a werewolf, something that shouldn't be happening. After running the werewolf off she meets Andreas Deluca, someone high up in the vampire counsel and also someone who appeals to her magic. It develops that there is many things going on including a drug war, attacks on people and who knows what else.<br />Ms Shields has done a very good job on developing a new twist on human/otherworlders stories. <div id="review_591566454" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591566454" />
    <a title="Kelly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5763047-kelly"><img alt="Kelly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578093823p2/5763047.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly" href="/user/show/5763047-kelly">Kelly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591566454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10991913671432136202">I have to admit, I was a little concerned starting the book. The story started with alot of imagery that and I was worried it was one of those books that described every small detail. But the truth is it set the stage for the story and dove right into the good stuff. You get an understanding of the young witch with an incredible amount of responsibility and power. Ari, the main character, is mature and levelheaded, with a good sense of humor. In addition to Ari, you meet Ryan her human counterpa</span>
  <span id="freeText10991913671432136202" style="display:none">I have to admit, I was a little concerned starting the book. The story started with alot of imagery that and I was worried it was one of those books that described every small detail. But the truth is it set the stage for the story and dove right into the good stuff. You get an understanding of the young witch with an incredible amount of responsibility and power. Ari, the main character, is mature and levelheaded, with a good sense of humor. In addition to Ari, you meet Ryan her human counterpart and Andreas, her vampire counterpart. You are brought into a world that supernatural beings coincide with humans. I found it very interesting that there were two factions of law enforcement, one for humans and one for the supernatural. The story is about cases that involve both, and how the two groups work together solving abnormal cases. I found this very entertaining and could not stop once I started reading this book. I was very happy to have the second book to continue the story. I am looking forward to reading more in this story. Ally Shields is definitely a writer to watch. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10991913671432136202" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14350284191501210833">In Riverdale, two communities live parallel lives – the world of humans and the Otherworld of vampires, witches, elves, nymphs and werecreatures. Ari is a Guardian. She is also a witch – but there is nothing twitchy-nosed about her. Ari is a special kind of law enforcer and when a horrific series of murders threatens all-out war in the Otherworld, she is the one that must lead the hunt, no matter what the cost… Ally Shields is a real find. She makes the implausible possible and creates a rollick</span>
  <span id="freeText14350284191501210833" style="display:none">In Riverdale, two communities live parallel lives – the world of humans and the Otherworld of vampires, witches, elves, nymphs and werecreatures. Ari is a Guardian. She is also a witch – but there is nothing twitchy-nosed about her. Ari is a special kind of law enforcer and when a horrific series of murders threatens all-out war in the Otherworld, she is the one that must lead the hunt, no matter what the cost… Ally Shields is a real find. She makes the implausible possible and creates a rollicking good story with strong characters, depth and atmosphere. Fantasy at its best and kept me turning the pages so that I read it all in one sitting as I couldn’t put it down. This is the first of a series and I can’t wait for the second part. Highly recommended.</span>

<div id="review_1593316406" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1593316406" />
    <a title="Naturalbri (Bri Wignall)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34041104-naturalbri-bri-wignall"><img alt="Naturalbri (Bri Wignall)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421149815p2/34041104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1593316406?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Naturalbri (Bri Wignall)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Naturalbri (Bri Wignall)" href="/user/show/34041104-naturalbri-bri-wignall">Naturalbri (Bri Wignall)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1593316406" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4438301734747766331">I loved this read! It was my first by this author and I cannot wait to read the rest of the series! If you are a fan of supernatural/paranormal and like when it mixes with the real world, this is going to rock your socks. <br/><br/>I thought the storyline was excellent. It was very unique, in both the plot and the way it was told. It mixed the real world and the imaginary very well, not giving us too much of either, but blending in a way that they were truly intermingled with one another. I also liked tha</span>
  <span id="freeText4438301734747766331" style="display:none">I loved this read! It was my first by this author and I cannot wait to read the rest of the series! If you are a fan of supernatural/paranormal and like when it mixes with the real world, this is going to rock your socks. <br /><br />I thought the storyline was excellent. It was very unique, in both the plot and the way it was told. It mixed the real world and the imaginary very well, not giving us too much of either, but blending in a way that they were truly intermingled with one another. I also liked that the story didn't just have one person who was working to fix the 'issue' and solve what is happening, it was a team and the team was a mixture of all sorts. <br /><br />The characters were developed brilliantly. There was depth, personality and a certain quirk about them that made me really connect with them. I liked that each was unique, but they still interacted, and even if they didn't always agree, they stuck together for the greater good. There were strong and intelligent characters leading the team, and they were passionate and empathetic. <br /><br />I found the pace really matched the story. We had fast paced sections, to really set apart the fact that there was a rush and a dire need to solve the crime and to find out who was behind it and why. There were also slower sections that really matched the fact that they needed to stop and think, to really breakdown what was taking place. I felt like this made it a lot more real. <br /><br />The story was easy to connect with and I really found myself hooked. I couldn't wait to get back and read more and now I find myself itching to dive into book two. <br /><br />I highly recommend this series. I think it is a brilliant book and I can tell that the rest of the series is going to continue to get even better. <br /><br />**I received this book for free in exchange for my honest an unbiased opinion. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4438301734747766331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_610906610" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610906610" />
    <a title="Chanzie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14188051-chanzie"><img alt="Chanzie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1516420945p2/14188051.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610906610?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chanzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chanzie" href="/user/show/14188051-chanzie">Chanzie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14188051-chanzie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14188051-chanzie?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14188051-chanzie?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610906610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11696617645328426092">Rating 3.5 / 5 stars<br/><br/>This is the second time reading Awakening the Fire. It really is amazing how much you don't pick up the first time you read a book, and it's so great how much more you notice the next time you read it. The book starts off with an intense and intriguing scene with Ari out on patrol as the Guardian of Olde Town. <br/><br/>Characters 3/5<br/>Ally creates well rounded and likable characters. There is some room for development but good grounding was formed in this book.<br/><br/>Ari - Ari is feisty and yo</span>
  <span id="freeText11696617645328426092" style="display:none">Rating 3.5 / 5 stars<br /><br />This is the second time reading Awakening the Fire. It really is amazing how much you don't pick up the first time you read a book, and it's so great how much more you notice the next time you read it. The book starts off with an intense and intriguing scene with Ari out on patrol as the Guardian of Olde Town. <br /><br />Characters 3/5<br />Ally creates well rounded and likable characters. There is some room for development but good grounding was formed in this book.<br /><br />Ari - Ari is feisty and you can connect with her easily. I find it amazing that she survives on so little sleep! She is a great heroine - she holds her own ground and doesn't swoon and fall over when she meets the hero of the book. I was very intrigued by her powers that are developing, and are yet to develop.<br /><br />Andreas - Andreas is smooth and charming. Even in the book he doesn't fit the stereotype of your typical vampire. He plays a low key role for the first half of the book and a much bigger role in second half. He is an intriguing and interesting character. I liked this character and am eager to see how he develops further in the series.<br /><br />Steffan - Steffan is your fun, friendly, fun to be around, nice guy/werewolf. He was my favourite character in the book. If Ari doesn't end up with Andreas, I hope she gives it a shot with Steffan!<br /><br />Plot, Pace &amp; Writing Style 4/5<br />You definitely ease into the story easily. Ally has a great easy writing style - the pace is great, the story has a very nice flow and the story has good world building. <br /><br />Cover talk 3/5 - I like the cover - It's got a nice paranormal feel to it and I love the purple flames!<br /><br />Final Thoughts: I will definitely continue with this series and have high hopes for it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11696617645328426092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kymmy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kymmy" href="/user/show/7394824-kymmy">Kymmy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer590460167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5750600324460435884">As a witch and the guardian in Riverdale, Arianna straddles the human world and the Otherworld of vampires, werewolves and things that go bump in the night. Working with a human cop, she tries to keep the peace between the worlds. This is hard to do when a new drug, affecting Otherworlders, shows up on the streets and humans and Otherworlders start dying.<br/>This urban fantasy was my first book by Ally Shields, but it will not be my last. Arianna reminded me of an early version of Anita Blake from L</span>
  <span id="freeText5750600324460435884" style="display:none">As a witch and the guardian in Riverdale, Arianna straddles the human world and the Otherworld of vampires, werewolves and things that go bump in the night. Working with a human cop, she tries to keep the peace between the worlds. This is hard to do when a new drug, affecting Otherworlders, shows up on the streets and humans and Otherworlders start dying.<br />This urban fantasy was my first book by Ally Shields, but it will not be my last. Arianna reminded me of an early version of Anita Blake from Laurell K. Hamilton's series. Her character was a take charge witch with a no nonsense attitude.<br />As the first book in the series, Ms. Shields had to set the stage for her readers. She made her characters interesting and likable. Arianna was a working girl with a lot of responsibility and stress on her shoulders. She takes her job seriously and it shows. She doesn't think she has time for romance until she meets a certain vampire and a dormant part of her magic is awakened.<br />If you like your urban fantasy with a dash of romance, Ms. Shields does not disappoint. The romance is on the back burner but it's there. I can't wait to see how Arianna grows as a fire witch or how she handles this fledging romantic relationship.<br />Do yourself a favor and read this book. The second book in the series, Fire Within, is already available. I'm looking forward to reading more of Arianna's story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5750600324460435884" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer591358177" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10675407400602261021">Awakening the Fire is a FANTASTIC book! It's the first in a series, and tells the story of Ari, a fire witch and Guardian in a world where humans live next to all sort of preternatural creatures. Her job is to keep the peace, but one night, Ari stumbles onto a werewolf attacking a couple of kids. She fights the werewolf off, saving the children, and shortly thereafter meets a vampire named Andreas. This coincidental meeting leads Ari onto a huge crime that is ongoing. As a cop, she investigates </span>
  <span id="freeText10675407400602261021" style="display:none">Awakening the Fire is a FANTASTIC book! It's the first in a series, and tells the story of Ari, a fire witch and Guardian in a world where humans live next to all sort of preternatural creatures. Her job is to keep the peace, but one night, Ari stumbles onto a werewolf attacking a couple of kids. She fights the werewolf off, saving the children, and shortly thereafter meets a vampire named Andreas. This coincidental meeting leads Ari onto a huge crime that is ongoing. As a cop, she investigates with the help of Andreas and many others, later discovering that the crimes are all part of something much larger than she ever dreamed.<br /><br />This book pulled me and didn't let go until the epilogue ended. I loved Ari and her determination to solve the crimes she was faced with. I also enjoyed her relationships with the other characters in the book. She is a strong heroine and easily moves the book along.<br /><br />I highly recommend Awakening the Fire to all urban fantasy/mystery fans, as well as anyone who enjoys strong characters and witty dialogue. This book is the newest addition to my keeper shelf!<br /><br />I give this book 5 stars and look forward to reading the next book in the series!<br /><br />Note: I was given a copy of this book for review purposes. This had no effect on my review.<br /><br />Note II: This review is cross-posted to Shelfari, Amazon, and Barnes &amp; Noble.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781939194268" href="/book/show/16498100-awakening-the-fire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3742922-susie?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer564719528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10783673991587383261">Awakening the Fire popped up on my radar after a GR friend reviewed it. It's been awhile since a new urban fantasy series has perked my interest. For being the first book in a series, I was surprised that there were very few things to become frustrated about. IMO, the author did a great job connecting me with the important characters, giving you a feel for the secondary characters, and gave enough information to give you a sense of the world. Just enough and not too overwhelming. <br/><br/>Some small comp</span>
  <span id="freeText10783673991587383261" style="display:none">Awakening the Fire popped up on my radar after a GR friend reviewed it. It's been awhile since a new urban fantasy series has perked my interest. For being the first book in a series, I was surprised that there were very few things to become frustrated about. IMO, the author did a great job connecting me with the important characters, giving you a feel for the secondary characters, and gave enough information to give you a sense of the world. Just enough and not too overwhelming. <br /><br />Some small complaints are references (not often) to things that mean nothing to me and doesn't quite explain what the big deal is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(i.e., ancient salamanders) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I'm sure we'll get a better idea in the books to come. <br /><br />As for the main character, I really like Ari. She doesn't seem too thickheaded and always out to prove to the world how tough and badass she is. Her inner dialogue makes her more relatable so I don't get too annoyed with her and her decisions. As for Andreas? He has me curious. I really like him and hope the two don't dance the "will they or won't they" for too long.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10783673991587383261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer479900302" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer677009773190508925">***Won this book in a first reads giveaway***<br/><br/>I really liked the world that they author created in this story and am looking forward to the next book in the series. I liked that you saw the steps in the investigation and it felt like a real investigation without magical leaps in order to solve the crimes. There were a lot of questions left up in the air, about Ari's powers. It would have been nice to have a few explanations about those powers and Andreas. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fTLezrtCVEqs1gXpFAChyOBopxlbOnjf2mJpxD9ty1Jdy2FubIqBpY0OCbFmF5NDi43CZq9TLitnncdwC/QaaA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MKpRQmfMunC1E/BMtaaANpyEw6QuKwTXmji/ARwi6okQU+7isARvn5TL/BTHsbK992Gm29pCUiMnxxG1KLs7sw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11634554577693650634">Ally Shields is the author of urban fantasy/paranormal mysteries with a touch of romance.<br/><br/>Her Guardian Witch series was completed in 2015 with the release of the seventh and final book, Eternal Fires. Due to an ongoing story line, Ms Shields recommends this series be read in order, beginning with Awakening the Fire. A series sequel of three books was completed in 2019.<br/><br/>The Elvenrude trilogy is set i</span>
  <span id="freeText11634554577693650634" style="display:none">Ally Shields is the author of urban fantasy/paranormal mysteries with a touch of romance.<br /><br />Her Guardian Witch series was completed in 2015 with the release of the seventh and final book, Eternal Fires. Due to an ongoing story line, Ms Shields recommends this series be read in order, beginning with Awakening the Fire. A series sequel of three books was completed in 2019.<br /><br />The Elvenrude trilogy is set in New Orleans and in an Elven world on the far side of a magic portal. It includes Cross Keys, an Elvenrude novel; Cross Keys: Revelation; and Cross Keys: Unity.<br /><br />The Maggie York Paranormal Mystery trilogy, also set in New Orleans, was completed in 2019.<br /><br />When not writing, Ms Shields reads multiple genres--urban fantasy, thrillers, mysteries, romance, and she loves to travel--anywhere, anytime.<br />She live in the Midwest within driving distance of the Mississippi River that is the setting for many of her fantasy stories.</span>
